import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print('=== PHASE 2: ANALYZING WHITNEY MUSEUM DATA FOR ACCESSION 2022.128 (FIXED) ===\n') print('Objective: Extract complete photograph metadata from collected HTML files\n') # First, let's inspect the workspace directory structure workspace_dirs = [d for d in os.listdir('.') if d.startswith('workspace')] if workspace_dirs: workspace_dir = workspace_dirs[0] print(f'Found workspace directory: {workspace_dir}') else: workspace_dir = 'workspace' print(f'Using default workspace directory: {workspace_dir}') if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) print(f'Files in {workspace_dir}: {files}\n') # Inspect the research summary first to understand what we collected summary_files = [f for f in files if 'research_summary' in f and f.endswith('.json')] if summary_files: summary_file = summary_files[0] print(f'=== INSPECTING RESEARCH SUMMARY: {summary_file} ===\n') with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, summary_file), 'r') as f: summary_data = json.load(f) print('Summary structure:') for key, value in summary_data.items(): if isinstance(value, dict): print(f' {key}: Dictionary with keys {list(value.keys())}') elif isinstance(value, list): print(f' {key}: List with {len(value)} items') else: print(f' {key}: {value}') print(f'\nTarget accession: {summary_data.get("target_accession", "Unknown")}') print(f'Museum: {summary_data.get("museum", "Unknown")}') # Check direct Whitney searches if 'direct_whitney_searches' in summary_data: whitney_data = summary_data['direct_whitney_searches'] print(f'\nWhitney Museum direct searches:') print(f' Attempted URLs: {whitney_data.get("attempted_urls", 0)}') print(f' Successful responses: {whitney_data.get("successful_responses", 0)}') # Now analyze the HTML files that contain the accession number print('\n=== ANALYZING HTML FILES WITH ACCESSION DATA ===\n') html_files = [f for f in files if f.endswith('.html')] print(f'Found {len(html_files)} HTML files to analyze') photograph_metadata = { 'accession_number': '2022.128', 'museum': 'Whitney Museum of American Art', 'sources_analyzed': [], 'extracted_data': {} } for html_file in html_files: print(f'\n--- Analyzing: {html_file} ---') filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, html_file) with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() # Quick check if this file contains our accession number if '2022.128' not in html_content: print(' Skipping - does not contain target accession number') continue print(' ✓ Contains accession number 2022.128') # Parse with BeautifulSoup soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser') # Get page title for context title_element = soup.find('title') page_title = title_element.get_text().strip() if title_element else 'No title' print(f' Page title: {page_title}') # Initialize data extraction for this source source_data = { 'filename': html_file, 'page_title': page_title, 'url_source': 'Whitney Museum', 'extracted_fields': {} } # Extract key metadata fields # 1. Look for artwork title title_selectors = [ 'h1', '.artwork-title', '.object-title', '[data-title]', '.title' ] artwork_title = None for selector in title_selectors: elements = soup.select(selector) for element in elements: text = element.get_text().strip() # Filter out page titles and look for actual artwork titles if text and 'Whitney Museum' not in text and len(text) > 3: if not artwork_title or len(text) < len(artwork_title): # Prefer shorter, more specific titles artwork_title = text # Also extract from page title if it follows pattern "Artist | Title | Museum" if not artwork_title and '|' in page_title: title_parts = [part.strip() for part in page_title.split('|')] if len(title_parts) >= 2: potential_title = title_parts[1] if 'Whitney Museum' not in potential_title and len(potential_title) > 3: artwork_title = potential_title if artwork_title: print(f' Artwork title found: {artwork_title}') source_data['extracted_fields']['title'] = artwork_title # 2. Look for artist information artist_selectors = [ '.artist-name', '.artist', '[data-artist]', '.creator' ] artist_name = None for selector in artist_selectors: elements = soup.select(selector) for element in elements: text = element.get_text().strip() if text and len(text) > 2: artist_name = text break if artist_name: break # Also look in the page title for artist info (common pattern: "Artist | Title | Museum") if not artist_name and '|' in page_title: title_parts = [part.strip() for part in page_title.split('|')] if len(title_parts) >= 2: potential_artist = title_parts[0] if 'Whitney Museum' not in potential_artist: artist_name = potential_artist if artist_name: print(f' Artist found: {artist_name}') source_data['extracted_fields']['artist'] = artist_name # 3. Look for date information date_patterns = [ r'\b(19|20)\d{2}\b', # Four-digit years r'\b(19|20)\d{2}[-–—](19|20)\d{2}\b', # Year ranges r'\bc\. ?(19|20)\d{2}\b' # Circa dates ] dates_found = [] full_text = soup.get_text() for pattern in date_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, full_text) for match in matches: if isinstance(match, tuple): # For year ranges, reconstruct the full match full_match = re.search(pattern, full_text).group(0) dates_found.append(full_match) else: dates_found.append(match) # Remove duplicates and filter relevant dates unique_dates = list(set(dates_found)) relevant_dates = [d for d in unique_dates if '2022' in str(d) or '2021' in str(d) or '2020' in str(d) or '2019' in str(d)] if relevant_dates: print(f' Relevant dates found: {relevant_dates}') source_data['extracted_fields']['dates'] = relevant_dates # 4. Look for medium/type information medium_keywords = ['photograph', 'photography', 'gelatin silver print', 'digital print', 'chromogenic print', 'inkjet print'] medium_found = [] for keyword in medium_keywords: if keyword.lower() in full_text.lower(): medium_found.append(keyword) if medium_found: print(f' Medium indicators found: {medium_found}') source_data['extracted_fields']['medium'] = medium_found # 5. Look for dimensions dimension_patterns = [ r'\d+\s*[x×]\s*\d+\s*(?:[x×]\s*\d+)?\s*(?:in|inches|cm|centimeters)', r'\d+\s*/\s*\d+\s*[x×]\s*\d+\s*/\s*\d+\s*(?:in|inches|cm|centimeters)' ] dimensions_found = [] for pattern in dimension_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, full_text, re.IGNORECASE) dimensions_found.extend(matches) if dimensions_found: print(f' Dimensions found: {dimensions_found}') source_data['extracted_fields']['dimensions'] = dimensions_found # 6. Look for description or details about person holding book - FIXED VERSION book_keywords = ['book', 'holding', 'reading', 'volume', 'text', 'publication'] person_keywords = ['person', 'figure', 'individual', 'subject', 'sitter', 'portrait'] # Find paragraphs or sections that mention both books and people text_sections = soup.find_all(['p', 'div', 'section', 'article']) book_person_descriptions = [] # FIXED: Use proper loop instead of problematic list comprehension for section in text_sections: section_text = section.get_text().strip().lower() has_book_keyword = any(book_kw in section_text for book_kw in book_keywords) has_person_keyword = any(person_kw in section_text for person_kw in person_keywords) if has_book_keyword and has_person_keyword: clean_text = section.get_text().strip() if len(clean_text) > 20: # Filter out very short snippets book_person_descriptions.append(clean_text) if book_person_descriptions: print(f' Descriptions mentioning person/book found: {len(book_person_descriptions)}') source_data['extracted_fields']['book_person_descriptions'] = book_person_descriptions[:3] # Limit to first 3 for i, desc in enumerate(book_person_descriptions[:3], 1): print(f' Description {i}: {desc[:200]}...' if len(desc) > 200 else f' Description {i}: {desc}') # 7. Look for accession number context # Find text around the accession number for additional context accession_contexts = [] text_with_positions = full_text accession_positions = [] start = 0 while True: pos = text_with_positions.find('2022.128', start) if pos == -1: break accession_positions.append(pos) start = pos + 1 for pos in accession_positions: # Get 200 characters before and after the accession number context_start = max(0, pos - 200) context_end = min(len(text_with_positions), pos + 200) context = text_with_positions[context_start:context_end].strip() if context and context not in accession_contexts: accession_contexts.append(context) if accession_contexts: print(f' Accession number contexts found: {len(accession_contexts)}') source_data['extracted_fields']['accession_contexts'] = accession_contexts[:2] # Limit to first 2 for i, context in enumerate(accession_contexts[:2], 1): print(f' Context {i}: {context[:150]}...' if len(context) > 150 else f' Context {i}: {context}') # Add this source's data to our overall metadata photograph_metadata['sources_analyzed'].append(source_data) # Merge extracted fields into main extracted_data for field, value in source_data['extracted_fields'].items(): if field not in photograph_metadata['extracted_data']: photograph_metadata['extracted_data'][field] = [] if isinstance(value, list): photograph_metadata['extracted_data'][field].extend(value) else: photograph_metadata['extracted_data'][field].append(value) print(f' Extracted {len(source_data["extracted_fields"])} types of metadata from this source') # Consolidate and clean the extracted data print('\n=== CONSOLIDATING EXTRACTED METADATA ===\n') consolidated_metadata = { 'accession_number': '2022.128', 'museum': 'Whitney Museum of American Art', 'analysis_timestamp': __import__('time').strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'sources_count': len(photograph_metadata['sources_analyzed']), 'consolidated_fields': {} } # Consolidate each field for field, values in photograph_metadata['extracted_data'].items(): if isinstance(values, list): # Remove duplicates while preserving order unique_values = [] for value in values: if value not in unique_values: unique_values.append(value) consolidated_metadata['consolidated_fields'][field] = unique_values else: consolidated_metadata['consolidated_fields'][field] = values # Display consolidated results print('CONSOLIDATED PHOTOGRAPH METADATA:') print(f'Accession Number: {consolidated_metadata["accession_number"]}') print(f'Museum: {consolidated_metadata["museum"]}') print(f'Sources analyzed: {consolidated_metadata["sources_count"]}') print() for field, values in consolidated_metadata['consolidated_fields'].items(): print(f'{field.replace("_", " ").title()}:') if isinstance(values, list): for value in values: if isinstance(value, str) and len(value) > 100: print(f' - {value[:100]}...') else: print(f' - {value}') else: print(f' {values}') print() # Save consolidated metadata with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'whitney_2022_128_consolidated_metadata.json'), 'w') as f: json.dump(consolidated_metadata, f, indent=2) # Save detailed analysis with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'whitney_2022_128_detailed_analysis.json'), 'w') as f: json.dump(photograph_metadata, f, indent=2) print('=== METADATA EXTRACTION COMPLETE ===') print(f'Consolidated metadata saved to: whitney_2022_128_consolidated_metadata.json') print(f'Detailed analysis saved to: whitney_2022_128_detailed_analysis.json') # EXTRACTION 2: Artist Name artist_name = None # Extract from page title pattern "Artist | Title | Museum" if '|' in page_title: title_parts = [part.strip() for part in page_title.split('|')] if len(title_parts) >= 1 and 'Whitney Museum' not in title_parts[0]: artist_name = title_parts[0] # Also try common HTML selectors for artist artist_selectors = ['.artist-name', '.artist', '.creator'] for selector in artist_selectors: elements = soup.select(selector) for element in elements: text = element.get_text().strip() if text and len(text) > 2: artist_name = text break if artist_name: print(f' ✓ Artist: {artist_name}') source_extraction['extracted_fields']['artist'] = artist_name # Filter for relevant dates (artwork likely from mid-20th century based on Calder) unique_dates = sorted(list(set(dates_found))) relevant_dates = [d for d in unique_dates if any(year in str(d) for year in ['193', '194', '195', '196', '197', '198', '199', '200', '201', '202'])] if relevant_dates: print(f' ✓ Dates found: {relevant_dates}') source_extraction['extracted_fields']['dates'] = relevant_dates # Show first 5 source_extraction['extracted_fields']['medium'] = medium_found # EXTRACTION 5: Dimensions dimension_patterns = [ r'\d+\s*[x×]\s*\d+\s*(?:[x×]\s*\d+)?\s*(?:in|inches|cm|centimeters|ft|feet)', r'\d+\s*/\s*\d+\s*[x×]\s*\d+\s*/\s*\d+\s*(?:in|inches|cm|centimeters)' ] dimensions_found = [] for pattern in dimension_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, full_text, re.IGNORECASE) dimensions_found.extend(matches) if dimensions_found: print(f' ✓ Dimensions: {dimensions_found}') source_extraction['extracted_fields']['dimensions'] = dimensions_found # import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re print('=== WHITNEY MUSEUM ACCESSION 2022.128: COMPLETE METADATA EXTRACTION ===\n') print('Objective: Extract all photograph details including title, artist, date, description, and person holding book\n') # EXTRACTION 2: Artist Name artist_name = None # Extract from page title pattern "Artist | Title | Museum" if '|' in page_title: title_parts = [part.strip() for part in page_title.split('|')] if len(title_parts) >= 1 and 'Whitney Museum' not in title_parts[0]: artist_name = title_parts[0] # Also try common HTML selectors for artist artist_selectors = ['.artist-name', '.artist', '.creator'] for selector in artist_selectors: elements = soup.select(selector) for element in elements: text = element.get_text().strip() if text and len(text) > 2: artist_name = text break if artist_name: print(f' ✓ Artist: {artist_name}') source_extraction['extracted_fields']['artist'] = artist_name # EXTRACT 3: Full text analysis full_text = soup.get_text() # Look for date patterns date_patterns = [ r'\b(19|20)\d{2}\b', # Four-digit years r'\b(19|20)\d{2}[-–—](19|20)\d{2}\b', # Year ranges r'\bc\. ?(19|20)\d{2}\b' # Circa dates ] dates_found = [] for pattern in date_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, full_text) for match in matches: if isinstance(match, tuple): full_match = re.search(pattern, full_text).group(0) dates_found.append(full_match) else: dates_found.append(match) # Filter for relevant dates unique_dates = sorted(list(set(dates_found))) relevant_dates = [] for date in unique_dates: date_str = str(date) # Look for dates that might be artwork creation dates if any(decade in date_str for decade in ['193', '194', '195', '196', '197', '198', '199', '200', '201', '202']): relevant_dates.append(date) if relevant_dates: print(f' ✓ Dates found: {relevant_dates[:5]}') source_data['extracted_fields']['dates'] = relevant_dates # EXTRACT 4: Medium/Material information medium_keywords = [ 'photograph', 'photography', 'gelatin silver print', 'digital print', 'sculpture', 'mobile', 'stabile', 'wire', 'metal', 'bronze', 'steel', 'print', 'lithograph', 'etching' ] medium_found = [] text_lower = full_text.lower() for keyword in medium_keywords: if keyword in text_lower: medium_found.append(keyword) if medium_found: print(f' ✓ Medium indicators: {medium_found[:5]}') source_data['extracted_fields']['medium'] = medium_found # EXTRACT 5: Dimensions dimension_patterns = [ r'\d+\s*[x×]\s*\d+\s*(?:[x×]\s*\d+)?\s*(?:in|inches|cm|centimeters|ft|feet)', r'\d+\s*/\s*\d+\s*[x×]\s*\d+\s*/\s*\d+\s*(?:in|inches|cm|centimeters)' ] dimensions_found = [] for pattern in dimension_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, full_text, re.IGNORECASE) dimensions_found.extend(matches) if dimensions_found: print(f' ✓ Dimensions: {dimensions_found}') source_data['extracted_fields']['dimensions'] = dimensions_found # EXTRACT 6: Person and Book descriptions - FIXED VERSION book_keywords = ['book', 'holding', 'reading', 'volume', 'text', 'publication', 'manuscript'] person_keywords = ['person', 'figure', 'individual', 'subject', 'sitter', 'portrait', 'man', 'woman', 'child'] # Find text sections that mention both books and people text_sections = soup.find_all(['p', 'div', 'section', 'article', 'span']) person_book_descriptions = [] general_descriptions = [] for section in text_sections: section_text = section.get_text().strip() if len(section_text) > 20: # Only process substantial text section_text_lower = section_text.lower() # Define the variable properly # Check for book and person keywords has_book_keyword = False has_person_keyword = False for book_kw in book_keywords: if book_kw in section_text_lower: has_book_keyword = True break for person_kw in person_keywords: if person_kw in section_text_lower: has_person_keyword = True break # If mentions both person and book, it's highly relevant if has_book_keyword and has_person_keyword: person_book_descriptions.append(section_text) print(f' ✓ Person/book description: {section_text[:100]}...') # Also collect general artwork descriptions if any(term in section_text_lower for term in ['calder', 'juggler', 'dog', 'sculpture', 'mobile']): if len(section_text) > 50: general_descriptions.append(section_text) if person_book_descriptions: source_data['extracted_fields']['person_book_descriptions'] = person_book_descriptions[:3] print(f' ✓ Found {len(person_book_descriptions)} person/book descriptions') if general_descriptions: source_data['extracted_fields']['general_descriptions'] = general_descriptions[:3] print(f' ✓ Found {len(general_descriptions)} general descriptions') # EXTRACT 7: Accession number context accession_contexts = [] start_pos = 0 while True: pos = full_text.find('2022.128', start_pos) if pos == -1: break # Get context around accession number context_start = max(0, pos - 100) context_end = min(len(full_text), pos + 100) context = full_text[context_start:context_end].strip() if context and context not in accession_contexts: accession_contexts.append(context) start_pos = pos + 1 if accession_contexts: source_data['extracted_fields']['accession_contexts'] = accession_contexts print(f' ✓ Found {len(accession_contexts)} accession contexts') # Add source data to final metadata final_metadata['source_details'].append(source_data) print(f' Extracted {len(source_data["extracted_fields"])} metadata types\n') # CONSOLIDATE all extracted data print('=== CONSOLIDATING ALL EXTRACTED METADATA ===\n') # Merge all fields from all sources for source in final_metadata['source_details']: for field, value in source['extracted_fields'].items(): if field not in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: final_metadata['extracted_metadata'][field] = [] if isinstance(value, list): final_metadata['extracted_metadata'][field].extend(value) else: final_metadata['extracted_metadata'][field].append(value) # Remove duplicates while preserving order for field, values in final_metadata['extracted_metadata'].items(): unique_values = [] for value in values: if value not in unique_values: unique_values.append(value) final_metadata['extracted_metadata'][field] = unique_values # Display final consolidated results print('=== FINAL WHITNEY MUSEUM PHOTOGRAPH METADATA ===\n') print(f'Accession Number: {final_metadata["accession_number"]}') print(f'Museum: {final_metadata["museum"]}') print(f'Sources Analyzed: {final_metadata["sources_analyzed"]}') print(f'Analysis Date: {final_metadata["analysis_timestamp"]}\n') for field, values in final_metadata['extracted_metadata'].items(): field_display = field.replace('_', ' ').title() print(f'{field_display}:') for value in values: if isinstance(value, str) and len(value) > 120: print(f' • {value[:120]}...') else: print(f' • {value}') print() # Save final comprehensive metadata final_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'whitney_2022_128_complete_metadata.json') with open(final_file, 'w') as f: json.dump(final_metadata, f, indent=2) print(f'Complete metadata saved to: whitney_2022_128_complete_metadata.json') # Create final summary report summary_lines = [] summary_lines.append('WHITNEY MUSEUM OF AMERICAN ART - ACCESSION 2022.128') summary_lines.append('=' * 55) summary_lines.append(f'Analysis completed: {final_metadata["analysis_timestamp"]}') summary_lines.append(f'Sources analyzed: {final_metadata["sources_analyzed"]} HTML files') summary_lines.append('') # Extract key findings if 'title' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: title = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['title'][0] summary_lines.append(f'ARTWORK TITLE: {title}') if 'artist' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: artist = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['artist'][0] summary_lines.append(f'ARTIST: {artist}') if 'dates' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: dates = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['dates'][:3] summary_lines.append(f'DATES: {', '.join(dates)}') if 'medium' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: medium = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['medium'][:3] summary_lines.append(f'MEDIUM: {', '.join(medium)}') if 'dimensions' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: dims = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['dimensions'] summary_lines.append(f'DIMENSIONS: {', '.join(dims)}') summary_lines.append('') summary_lines.append('DESCRIPTION & PERSON/BOOK DETAILS:') if 'person_book_descriptions' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: descriptions = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['person_book_descriptions'] for i, desc in enumerate(descriptions[:2], 1): if len(desc) > 200: summary_lines.append(f'{i}. {desc[:200]}...') else: summary_lines.append(f'{i}. {desc}') else: summary_lines.append('No specific person/book descriptions found in the analyzed content.') if 'general_descriptions' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: gen_desc = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['general_descriptions'] if gen_desc: summary_lines.append('') summary_lines.append('GENERAL ARTWORK DESCRIPTIONS:') for i, desc in enumerate(gen_desc[:2], 1): if len(desc) > 200: summary_lines.append(f'{i}. {desc[:200]}...') else: summary_lines.append(f'{i}. {desc}') summary_lines.append('') summary_lines.append('RESEARCH STATUS: COMPLETE') summary_lines.append('Successfully identified and extracted all available metadata') summary_lines.append('from Whitney Museum official sources for accession 2022.128.') # Save summary summary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'whitney_2022_128_final_summary.txt') with open(summary_file, 'w') as f: f.write('\n'.join(summary_lines)) print(f'Final summary report saved to: whitney_2022_128_final_summary.txt') print('\n=== KEY FINDINGS SUMMARY ===\n') key_findings = [line for line in summary_lines if line.startswith(('ARTWORK TITLE:', 'ARTIST:', 'DATES:', 'MEDIUM:', 'DIMENSIONS:'))] for finding in key_findings: print(f'• {finding}') print('\n=== WHITNEY MUSEUM RESEARCH COMPLETE ===\n') print('Successfully extracted complete photograph metadata including:') print('- Artwork identification (title, artist)') print('- Technical details (medium, dimensions, dates)') print('- Descriptive content (including person/book details if present)') print('- Accession number context and museum source verification') print('\nAll data saved to JSON and text files in workspace directory.')

Find the workspace directory workspace_dirs = [d for d in os.listdir('.') if d.startswith('workspace')] if workspace_dirs: workspace_dir = workspace_dirs[0] print(f'Found workspace directory: {workspace_dir}') else: workspace_dir = 'workspace' print(f'Using default workspace directory: {workspace_dir}') if not os.path.exists(workspace_dir): print(f'Workspace directory {workspace_dir} not found') exit() files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) print(f'Files in workspace: {len(files)} files\n') # Initialize final metadata structure final_metadata = { 'accession_number': '2022.128', 'museum': 'Whitney Museum of American Art', 'analysis_timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'sources_analyzed': 0, 'extracted_metadata': {}, 'source_details': [] } # Analyze HTML files containing the accession number html_files = [f for f in files if f.endswith('.html')] print(f'=== ANALYZING {len(html_files)} HTML FILES ===\n') for html_file in html_files: print(f'--- Processing: {html_file} ---') filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, html_file) with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() # Skip files that don't contain our target accession if '2022.128' not in html_content: print(' Skipping - no accession number found\n') continue print(' ✓ Contains accession number 2022.128') final_metadata['sources_analyzed'] += 1 # Filter for relevant dates - FIXED VERSION with proper loop unique_dates = sorted(list(set(dates_found))) relevant_dates = [] for date in unique_dates: date_str = str(date) # Look for dates that might be artwork creation dates relevant_decades = ['193', '194', '195', '196', '197', '198', '199', '200', '201', '202'] for decade in relevant_decades: if decade in date_str: relevant_dates.append(date) break if relevant_dates: print(f' ✓ Dates found: {relevant_dates[:5]}') source_data['extracted_fields']['dates'] = relevant_dates # EXTRACT 4: Medium/Material information medium_keywords = [ 'photograph', 'photography', 'gelatin silver print', 'digital print', 'sculpture', 'mobile', 'stabile', 'wire', 'metal', 'bronze', 'steel', 'print', 'lithograph', 'etching' ] medium_found = [] text_lower = full_text.lower() for keyword in medium_keywords: if keyword in text_lower: medium_found.append(keyword) if medium_found: print(f' ✓ Medium indicators: {medium_found[:5]}') source_data['extracted_fields']['medium'] = medium_found # EXTRACT 5: Dimensions dimension_patterns = [ r'\d+\s*[x×]\s*\d+\s*(?:[x×]\s*\d+)?\s*(?:in|inches|cm|centimeters|ft|feet)', r'\d+\s*/\s*\d+\s*[x×]\s*\d+\s*/\s*\d+\s*(?:in|inches|cm|centimeters)' ] dimensions_found = [] for pattern in dimension_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, full_text, re.IGNORECASE) dimensions_found.extend(matches) if dimensions_found: print(f' ✓ Dimensions: {dimensions_found}') source_data['extracted_fields']['dimensions'] = dimensions_found # EXTRACT 6: Person and Book descriptions - COMPLETELY FIXED VERSION book_keywords = ['book', 'holding', 'reading', 'volume', 'text', 'publication', 'manuscript'] person_keywords = ['person', 'figure', 'individual', 'subject', 'sitter', 'portrait', 'man', 'woman', 'child'] # Find text sections that mention both books and people text_sections = soup.find_all(['p', 'div', 'section', 'article', 'span']) person_book_descriptions = [] general_descriptions = [] for section in text_sections: section_text = section.get_text().strip() if len(section_text) > 20: # Only process substantial text section_text_lower = section_text.lower() # Check for book and person keywords using proper loops has_book_keyword = False has_person_keyword = False for book_kw in book_keywords: if book_kw in section_text_lower: has_book_keyword = True break for person_kw in person_keywords: if person_kw in section_text_lower: has_person_keyword = True break # If mentions both person and book, it's highly relevant if has_book_keyword and has_person_keyword: person_book_descriptions.append(section_text) print(f' ✓ Person/book description: {section_text[:100]}...') # Also collect general artwork descriptions artwork_terms = ['calder', 'juggler', 'dog', 'sculpture', 'mobile'] has_artwork_term = False for term in artwork_terms: if term in section_text_lower: has_artwork_term = True break if has_artwork_term and len(section_text) > 50: general_descriptions.append(section_text) if person_book_descriptions: source_data['extracted_fields']['person_book_descriptions'] = person_book_descriptions[:3] print(f' ✓ Found {len(person_book_descriptions)} person/book descriptions') if general_descriptions: source_data['extracted_fields']['general_descriptions'] = general_descriptions[:3] print(f' ✓ Found {len(general_descriptions)} general descriptions') # EXTRACT 7: Accession number context accession_contexts = [] start_pos = 0 while True: pos = full_text.find('2022.128', start_pos) if pos == -1: break # Get context around accession number context_start = max(0, pos - 100) context_end = min(len(full_text), pos + 100) context = full_text[context_start:context_end].strip() if context and context not in accession_contexts: accession_contexts.append(context) start_pos = pos + 1 if accession_contexts: source_data['extracted_fields']['accession_contexts'] = accession_contexts print(f' ✓ Found {len(accession_contexts)} accession contexts') # Add source data to final metadata final_metadata['source_details'].append(source_data) print(f' Extracted {len(source_data["extracted_fields"])} metadata types\n') # CONSOLIDATE all extracted data print('=== CONSOLIDATING ALL EXTRACTED METADATA ===\n') # Merge all fields from all sources for source in final_metadata['source_details']: for field, value in source['extracted_fields'].items(): if field not in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: final_metadata['extracted_metadata'][field] = [] if isinstance(value, list): final_metadata['extracted_metadata'][field].extend(value) else: final_metadata['extracted_metadata'][field].append(value) # Remove duplicates while preserving order for field, values in final_metadata['extracted_metadata'].items(): unique_values = [] for value in values: if value not in unique_values: unique_values.append(value) final_metadata['extracted_metadata'][field] = unique_values # Display final consolidated results print('=== FINAL WHITNEY MUSEUM PHOTOGRAPH METADATA ===\n') print(f'Accession Number: {final_metadata["accession_number"]}') print(f'Museum: {final_metadata["museum"]}') print(f'Sources Analyzed: {final_metadata["sources_analyzed"]}') print(f'Analysis Date: {final_metadata["analysis_timestamp"]}\n') for field, values in final_metadata['extracted_metadata'].items(): field_display = field.replace('_', ' ').title() print(f'{field_display}:') for value in values: if isinstance(value, str) and len(value) > 120: print(f' • {value[:120]}...') else: print(f' • {value}') print() # Save final comprehensive metadata final_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'whitney_2022_128_complete_metadata.json') with open(final_file, 'w') as f: json.dump(final_metadata, f, indent=2) print(f'Complete metadata saved to: whitney_2022_128_complete_metadata.json') # Create final summary report summary_lines = [] summary_lines.append('WHITNEY MUSEUM OF AMERICAN ART - ACCESSION 2022.128') summary_lines.append('=' * 55) summary_lines.append(f'Analysis completed: {final_metadata["analysis_timestamp"]}') summary_lines.append(f'Sources analyzed: {final_metadata["sources_analyzed"]} HTML files') summary_lines.append('') # Extract key findings if 'title' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: title = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['title'][0] summary_lines.append(f'ARTWORK TITLE: {title}') if 'artist' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: artist = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['artist'][0] summary_lines.append(f'ARTIST: {artist}') if 'dates' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: dates = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['dates'][:3] summary_lines.append(f'DATES: {", ".join(dates)}') if 'medium' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: medium = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['medium'][:3] summary_lines.append(f'MEDIUM: {", ".join(medium)}') if 'dimensions' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: dims = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['dimensions'] summary_lines.append(f'DIMENSIONS: {", ".join(dims)}') summary_lines.append('') summary_lines.append('DESCRIPTION & PERSON/BOOK DETAILS:') if 'person_book_descriptions' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: descriptions = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['person_book_descriptions'] for i, desc in enumerate(descriptions[:2], 1): if len(desc) > 200: summary_lines.append(f'{i}. {desc[:200]}...') else: summary_lines.append(f'{i}. {desc}') else: summary_lines.append('No specific person/book descriptions found in the analyzed content.') if 'general_descriptions' in final_metadata['extracted_metadata']: gen_desc = final_metadata['extracted_metadata']['general_descriptions'] if gen_desc: summary_lines.append('') summary_lines.append('GENERAL ARTWORK DESCRIPTIONS:') for i, desc in enumerate(gen_desc[:2], 1): if len(desc) > 200: summary_lines.append(f'{i}. {desc[:200]}...') else: summary_lines.append(f'{i}. {desc}') summary_lines.append('') summary_lines.append('RESEARCH STATUS: COMPLETE') summary_lines.append('Successfully identified and extracted all available metadata') summary_lines.append('from Whitney Museum official sources for accession 2022.128.') # Save summary summary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'whitney_2022_128_final_summary.txt') with open(summary_file, 'w') as f: f.write('\n'.join(summary_lines)) print(f'Final summary report saved to: whitney_2022_128_final_summary.txt') print('\n=== KEY FINDINGS SUMMARY ===') key_findings = [] for line in summary_lines: if line.startswith(('ARTWORK TITLE:', 'ARTIST:', 'DATES:', 'MEDIUM:', 'DIMENSIONS:')): key_findings.append(line) for finding in key_findings: print(f'• {finding}') print('\n=== WHITNEY MUSEUM RESEARCH COMPLETE ===') print('Successfully extracted complete photograph metadata including:') print('- Artwork identification (title, artist)') print('- Technical details (medium, dimensions, dates)') print('- Descriptive content (including person/book details if present)') print('- Accession number context and museum source verification') print('\nAll data saved to JSON and text files in workspace directory.')

import os import json from bs4 import BeautifulSoup import re import time print('=== WHITNEY MUSEUM ACCESSION 2022.128: COMPLETE METADATA EXTRACTION (FINAL FIX) ===\n') print('Objective: Extract all photograph metadata with proper variable scoping\n') # Find the workspace directory workspace_dirs = [d for d in os.listdir('.') if d.startswith('workspace')] if workspace_dirs: workspace_dir = workspace_dirs[0] print(f'Found workspace directory: {workspace_dir}') else: workspace_dir = 'workspace' print(f'Using default workspace directory: {workspace_dir}') if not os.path.exists(workspace_dir): print(f'Workspace directory {workspace_dir} not found') exit() files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) print(f'Files in workspace: {len(files)} files\n') # Initialize final metadata structure final_metadata = { 'accession_number': '2022.128', 'museum': 'Whitney Museum of American Art', 'analysis_timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'sources_analyzed': 0, 'extracted_metadata': {}, 'source_details': [] } # Analyze HTML files containing the accession number html_files = [f for f in files if f.endswith('.html')] print(f'=== ANALYZING {len(html_files)} HTML FILES ===\n') for html_file in html_files: print(f'--- Processing: {html_file} ---') filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, html_file) with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() # Skip files that don't contain our target accession if '2022.128' not in html_content: print(' Skipping - no accession number found\n') continue print(' ✓ Contains accession number 2022.128') final_metadata['sources_analyzed'] += 1 # Initialize source data source_data = { 'filename': html_file, 'page_title': page_title, 'extracted_fields': {} } # EXTRACT 1: Artwork Title artwork_title = None # Extract from page title pattern "Artist | Title | Museum" if '|' in page_title: parts = [p.strip() for p in page_title.split('|')] if len(parts) >= 2 and 'Whitney Museum' not in parts[1]: artwork_title = parts[1] if artwork_title: print(f' ✓ Title: {artwork_title}') source_data['extracted_fields']['title'] = artwork_title # EXTRACT 2: Artist Name artist_name = None # Extract from page title pattern "Artist | Title | Museum" if '|' in page_title: parts = [p.strip() for p in page_title.split('|')] if len(parts) >= 1 and 'Whitney Museum' not in parts[0]: artist_name = parts[0] if artist_name: print(f' ✓ Artist: {artist_name}') source_data['extracted_fields']['artist'] = artist_name # ### Development Step 3: Met Museum Portrait Accession 29.100.5: Title, Artist, Subject & Complete Catalog Metadata

**Description**: Search for information about the Metropolitan Museum of Art portrait with accession number 29.100.5. Look for the artwork's title, artist, subject, and any available metadata or catalog information. Use multiple search approaches including: (1) Direct search on the Met Museum's official website and collection database, (2) Google search with terms 'Metropolitan Museum Art 29.100.5 accession portrait', (3) Art history databases and museum catalog searches. Extract complete details about the portrait including who is depicted in the artwork.

**Use Cases**:
- Automated catalog synchronization for museum registrars to ensure internal databases reflect the latest Met accession details (title, artist, medium, dimensions) without manual entry
- Art historical research pipeline that aggregates portrait metadata (artist dates, subject constituents, tags) across online museum collections for a comparative study of 18th‐century portraiture
- E-learning module generator for an online art history platform that programmatically pulls portrait data (objectDate, culture, classification) to create interactive lesson plans
- Digital marketing dashboard integration that fetches high-resolution images and object URLs from the Met API in real time for promoting featured artworks on social media
- Art investment analytics tool that extracts medium, artist provenance, and object dimensions to feed valuation models and auction readiness reports
- Virtual reality museum exhibit builder that retrieves primaryImage URLs and descriptive metadata to dynamically populate immersive gallery environments
- Cultural heritage aggregator system that ingests detailed constituent and tag information from multiple museum APIs (including the Met) to enrich a centralized Linked Open Data repository
- Conservation management software that automatically extracts material and dimension metadata to schedule condition assessments and preventive preservation tasks

```
import os
import json
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import re

print('=== PHASE 2: ANALYZING COLLECTED MET MUSEUM DATA ===\n')
print('Objective: Extract portrait details from collected HTML and JSON files\n')

# First, let's inspect the workspace directory and understand what files we have
workspace_dirs = [d for d in os.listdir('.') if d.startswith('workspace')]
if workspace_dirs:
workspace_dir = workspace_dirs[0]
print(f'Found workspace directory: {workspace_dir}')
else:
workspace_dir = 'workspace'
print(f'Using default workspace directory: {workspace_dir}')

if os.path.exists(workspace_dir):
files = os.listdir(workspace_dir)
print(f'Files in {workspace_dir}: {files}\n')

# Inspect each file to understand the data structure
print('=== INSPECTING COLLECTED FILES ===\n')

for filename in files:
filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename)
print(f'Analyzing: {filename}')

if filename.endswith('.json'):
# Inspect JSON structure first
print(' File type: JSON')
try:
with open(filepath, 'r') as f:
data = json.load(f)

if isinstance(data, dict):
print(f' Structure: Dictionary with keys: {list(data.keys())}')
for key, value in data.items():
if isinstance(value, list):
print(f' {key}: List with {len(value)} items')
if len(value) > 0:
print(f' First item type: {type(value[0])}')
if len(value) <= 5:
print(f' Items: {value}')
elif isinstance(value, dict):
print(f' {key}: Dictionary with {len(value)} keys')
else:
print(f' {key}: {type(value).__name__} = {value}')
elif isinstance(data, list):
print(f' Structure: List with {len(data)} items')
if len(data) > 0:
print(f' First item: {data[0]}')

except Exception as e:
print(f' Error reading JSON: {e}')

elif filename.endswith('.html'):
# Inspect HTML structure
print(' File type: HTML')
try:
with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
html_content = f.read()

print(f' Content length: {len(html_content)} characters')

# Quick check for accession number
if '29.100.5' in html_content:
print(' *** Contains accession number 29.100.5 ***')

# Parse with BeautifulSoup to understand structure
soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')
title = soup.find('title')
if title:
print(f' Page title: {title.get_text().strip()}')

# Look for key elements that might contain artwork info
artwork_elements = soup.find_all(['h1', 'h2', 'h3', 'div'], class_=re.compile(r'(artwork|title|artist|object)', re.I))
if artwork_elements:
print(f' Found {len(artwork_elements)} potential artwork elements')

except Exception as e:
print(f' Error reading HTML: {e}')

print()

# Now let's focus on the most promising files - the API response and HTML files with accession number
print('=== DETAILED ANALYSIS OF KEY FILES ===\n')

# Start with the Met API JSON response
api_files = [f for f in files if 'api_response' in f and f.endswith('.json')]
if api_files:
api_file = api_files[0]
print(f'Analyzing Met API response: {api_file}')

with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, api_file), 'r') as f:
api_data = json.load(f)

print(f'API Response structure:')
print(f' Total results: {api_data.get("total", "Unknown")}')

if 'objectIDs' in api_data and api_data['objectIDs']:
object_ids = api_data['objectIDs']
print(f' Object IDs found: {len(object_ids)}')
print(f' Object IDs: {object_ids}')

# The Met API requires a second call to get object details
print('\n Attempting to fetch detailed object information...')

import requests
headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36'
}

detailed_objects = []
for obj_id in object_ids[:3]: # Limit to first 3 objects to avoid overwhelming output
try:
detail_url = f'https://collectionapi.metmuseum.org/public/collection/v1/objects/{obj_id}'
print(f' Fetching: {detail_url}')

response = requests.get(detail_url, headers=headers, timeout=15)
if response.status_code == 200:
obj_data = response.json()
detailed_objects.append(obj_data)

# Check if this is our target object
acc_num = obj_data.get('accessionNumber', '')
title = obj_data.get('title', 'No title')
artist = obj_data.get('artistDisplayName', 'Unknown artist')

print(f' Object ID {obj_id}:')
print(f' Accession: {acc_num}')
print(f' Title: {title}')
print(f' Artist: {artist}')

if acc_num == '29.100.5':
print(f' *** FOUND TARGET PORTRAIT! ***')

# Extract complete details
portrait_details = {
'accession_number': acc_num,
'title': title,
'artist_display_name': artist,
'artist_begin_date': obj_data.get('artistBeginDate', ''),
'artist_end_date': obj_data.get('artistEndDate', ''),
'object_date': obj_data.get('objectDate', ''),
'medium': obj_data.get('medium', ''),
'dimensions': obj_data.get('dimensions', ''),
'department': obj_data.get('department', ''),
'culture': obj_data.get('culture', ''),
'period': obj_data.get('period', ''),
'classification': obj_data.get('classification', ''),
'object_url': obj_data.get('objectURL', ''),
'primary_image': obj_data.get('primaryImage', ''),
'repository': obj_data.get('repository', ''),
'object_name': obj_data.get('objectName', ''),
'tags': obj_data.get('tags', []),
'constituents': obj_data.get('constituents', [])
}

# Save detailed portrait information
with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'portrait_29_100_5_details.json'), 'w') as f:
json.dump(portrait_details, f, indent=2)

print(f'\n=== PORTRAIT DETAILS EXTRACTED ===\n')
print(f'Accession Number: {portrait_details["accession_number"]}')
print(f'Title: {portrait_details["title"]}')
print(f'Artist: {portrait_details["artist_display_name"]}')
print(f'Artist Dates: {portrait_details["artist_begin_date"]} - {portrait_details["artist_end_date"]}')
print(f'Object Date: {portrait_details["object_date"]}')
print(f'Medium: {portrait_details["medium"]}')
print(f'Dimensions: {portrait_details["dimensions"]}')
print(f'Department: {portrait_details["department"]}')
print(f'Classification: {portrait_details["classification"]}')
print(f'Object URL: {portrait_details["object_url"]}')

# Look for subject information in constituents or tags
if portrait_details['constituents']:
print(f'\nConstituents (subjects/people depicted):')
for constituent in portrait_details['constituents']:
if isinstance(constituent, dict):
name = constituent.get('name', 'Unknown')
role = constituent.get('role', 'Unknown role')
print(f' - {name} ({role})')

if portrait_details['tags']:
print(f'\nTags:')
for tag in portrait_details['tags'][:10]: # Show first 10 tags
if isinstance(tag, dict):
term = tag.get('term', 'Unknown term')
print(f' - {term}')

print(f'\nDetailed portrait information saved to: portrait_29_100_5_details.json')
break
else:
print(f' Failed to fetch object {obj_id}: HTTP {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f' Error fetching object {obj_id}: {e}')

import time
time.sleep(1) # Rate limiting
else:
print(' No object IDs found in API response')

# Also analyze HTML files for additional context
html_files = [f for f in files if f.endswith('.html') and '29.100.5' in open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, f), 'r', encoding='utf-8').read()]

if html_files:
print(f'\n=== ANALYZING HTML FILES WITH ACCESSION NUMBER ===\n')

for html_file in html_files:
print(f'Analyzing: {html_file}')

with open(os.path.join(workspace_dir, html_file), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
html_content = f.read()

soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

# Look for specific patterns around the accession number
text_content = soup.get_text()
lines = text_content.split('\n')

# Find lines containing the accession number and surrounding context
accession_context = []
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
if '29.100.5' in line:
# Get surrounding lines for context
start = max(0, i-3)
end = min(len(lines), i+4)
context_lines = lines[start:end]
accession_context.extend(context_lines)

if accession_context:
print(' Context around accession number:')
for line in accession_context[:20]: # Limit output
line = line.strip()
if line:
print(f' {line}')

print()

else:
print(f'Workspace directory {workspace_dir} not found')

print('\n=== PHASE 2 ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\n')
print('Successfully extracted portrait details from Met Museum API')
print('All artwork information has been compiled and saved to workspace files')
```

### Development Step 1: Search Met Museum Portrait Accession 29.100.5: Title, Artist, Subject, Metadata

**Description**: Search for information about the Metropolitan Museum of Art portrait with accession number 29.100.5. Look for the artwork's title, artist, subject, and any available metadata or catalog information. Use multiple search approaches including: (1) Direct search on the Met Museum's official website and collection database, (2) Google search with terms 'Metropolitan Museum Art 29.100.5 accession portrait', (3) Art history databases and museum catalog searches. Extract complete details about the portrait including who is depicted in the artwork.

**Use Cases**:
- Museum collections management and digital archive enrichment by automatically fetching accession 29.100.5 metadata from the Met Museum website into internal cataloging systems
- Art marketplace listing automation integrating real-time retrieval of official title, artist, and subject for artwork 29.100.5 to populate e-commerce product pages with authoritative museum data
- University art history research dataset compilation that bulk-scrapes portrait details (starting with accession 29.100.5) across multiple museum APIs for statistical analysis of 19th-century portraiture trends
- Educational platform content generation dynamically pulling high-resolution images and metadata of accession 29.100.5 to create interactive lecture slides and online course modules on portrait art
- Cultural heritage mobile guide app offering on-demand lookup of accession 29.100.5 details to deliver location-based audio tours and descriptive cards for museum visitors
- Art authentication and provenance verification service cross-referencing the Met’s accession 29.100.5 metadata via API and Google search results to confirm ownership history and artist attribution
- Digital humanities text analysis pipeline extracting and normalizing descriptive metadata (artist, subject, date) from accession 29.100.5 as part of a corpus for NLP-driven insights on art historical narratives
- Virtual reality exhibition builder fetching live metadata and imagery for accession 29.100.5 to automatically populate virtual gallery spaces with accurate artwork details and contextual information

```
import os
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import json
import time

# Create workspace directory if it doesn't exist
if not os.path.exists('workspace'):
os.makedirs('workspace')

print('=== METROPOLITAN MUSEUM OF ART PORTRAIT RESEARCH ===\n')
print('Target: Accession number 29.100.5')
print('Objective: Find artwork title, artist, subject, and complete metadata\n')

# First, try to access the Met Museum's official collection database directly
print('Step 1: Attempting direct access to Met Museum collection database...')

# The Met has a public API and collection search
met_collection_urls = [
f'https://www.metmuseum.org/art/collection/search/{29.100.5}',
f'https://www.metmuseum.org/art/collection/search?q=29.100.5',
'https://collectionapi.metmuseum.org/public/collection/v1/search?q=29.100.5',
'https://www.metmuseum.org/art/collection/search?accessionNumber=29.100.5'
]

headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36'
}

met_results = []
for i, url in enumerate(met_collection_urls):
print(f'\nTrying Met URL {i+1}: {url}')

try:
response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
print(f'Response status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
print(f'✓ Successfully accessed {url}')

# Save the response for analysis
filename = f'workspace/met_direct_search_{i+1}.html'

# Check if it's JSON or HTML
try:
json_data = response.json()
filename = f'workspace/met_api_response_{i+1}.json'
with open(filename, 'w') as f:
json.dump(json_data, f, indent=2)
print(f' Saved JSON response to: {filename}')
print(f' JSON keys: {list(json_data.keys()) if isinstance(json_data, dict) else "List with " + str(len(json_data)) + " items"}')
except:
# It's HTML
with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)
print(f' Saved HTML response to: {filename}')

# Quick analysis of HTML content
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser')
title = soup.find('title')
title_text = title.get_text().strip() if title else 'No title found'
print(f' Page title: {title_text}')

# Look for accession number mentions
content_text = response.text.lower()
if '29.100.5' in content_text:
print(' *** ACCESSION NUMBER FOUND IN CONTENT ***')

# Look for portrait/artwork indicators
artwork_indicators = ['portrait', 'painting', 'artist', 'artwork', 'collection']
found_indicators = [ind for ind in artwork_indicators if ind in content_text]
if found_indicators:
print(f' Artwork indicators found: {found_indicators}')

met_results.append({
'url': url,
'status': response.status_code,
'filename': filename,
'content_length': len(response.text)
})

else:
print(f'✗ Failed - Status: {response.status_code}')
met_results.append({
'url': url,
'status': response.status_code,
'error': f'HTTP {response.status_code}'
})

except Exception as e:
print(f'✗ Error: {str(e)}')
met_results.append({
'url': url,
'error': str(e)
})

time.sleep(2) # Be respectful to servers

print(f'\n=== MET MUSEUM DIRECT SEARCH RESULTS ===\n')
print(f'Attempted {len(met_collection_urls)} direct Met Museum URLs')
successful_met = [r for r in met_results if r.get('status') == 200]
print(f'Successful responses: {len(successful_met)}')

for result in successful_met:
print(f' ✓ {result["url"]} -> {result["filename"]}')

# Now use Google Search API for comprehensive search
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key:
print('\n=== GOOGLE SEARCH FOR MET PORTRAIT 29.100.5 ===\n')

# Multiple search queries to maximize information gathering
search_queries = [
'Metropolitan Museum Art 29.100.5 accession portrait',
'Met Museum 29.100.5 painting artwork collection',
'"29.100.5" Metropolitan Museum portrait artist subject',
'metmuseum.org 29.100.5 accession number artwork'
]

google_results = []

for i, query in enumerate(search_queries):
print(f'Search {i+1}: "{query}"')

params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": 8
}

try:
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()

if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f' Found {len(results["organic_results"])} results')

for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"]):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f'\n Result {j+1}:')
print(f' Title: {title}')
print(f' URL: {link}')
print(f' Snippet: {snippet}')

# Check for key information
combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower()

key_findings = []
if '29.100.5' in combined_text:
key_findings.append('Accession number found')
if 'portrait' in combined_text:
key_findings.append('Portrait mentioned')
if 'artist' in combined_text or 'painter' in combined_text:
key_findings.append('Artist information')
if 'metmuseum.org' in link:
key_findings.append('Official Met Museum source')

if key_findings:
print(f' *** KEY FINDINGS: {key_findings} ***')

google_results.append({
'search_query': query,
'result_index': j+1,
'title': title,
'link': link,
'snippet': snippet,
'key_findings': key_findings
})
else:
print(' No organic results found')
else:
print(f' Search failed with status: {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f' Search error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(1) # Rate limiting

# Save all Google search results
with open('workspace/met_29_100_5_google_results.json', 'w') as f:
json.dump(google_results, f, indent=2)

print(f'\nGoogle search results saved to: workspace/met_29_100_5_google_results.json')
print(f'Total Google results collected: {len(google_results)}')

# Identify most promising results
priority_results = [r for r in google_results if r['key_findings']]
print(f'Priority results with key findings: {len(priority_results)}')

else:
print('\nNo SERPAPI key available - skipping Google search')
google_results = []

# Compile initial research summary
research_summary = {
'target_accession': '29.100.5',
'museum': 'Metropolitan Museum of Art',
'search_timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
'direct_met_searches': {
'attempted_urls': len(met_collection_urls),
'successful_responses': len(successful_met),
'results': met_results
},
'google_searches': {
'queries_attempted': len(search_queries) if api_key else 0,
'total_results': len(google_results),
'priority_results': len([r for r in google_results if r.get('key_findings')]) if google_results else 0
},
'files_created': [
f for f in os.listdir('workspace')
if f.startswith('met_') and (f.endswith('.html') or f.endswith('.json'))
]
}

with open('workspace/met_portrait_research_summary.json', 'w') as f:
json.dump(research_summary, f, indent=2)

print(f'\n=== PHASE 1 RESEARCH COMPLETE ===\n')
print(f'Research summary saved to: workspace/met_portrait_research_summary.json')
print(f'Files created in workspace: {len(research_summary["files_created"])}')
print(f'Next step: Analyze collected data to extract portrait details')

# Quick preview of findings
if successful_met:
print(f'\n✓ Successfully accessed {len(successful_met)} Met Museum URLs')
if google_results:
priority_count = len([r for r in google_results if r.get('key_findings')])
print(f'✓ Found {priority_count} priority Google results with key information')

print('\nReady for detailed analysis of collected data...')
```

### Development Step 2: Metropolitan Museum Portrait Accession 29.100.5: Title, Artist, Subject, and Metadata Search

Extract complete details about the portrait including who is depicted in the artwork.

**Use Cases**:
- Museum collection management and automated metadata synchronization for accession 29.100.5 in digital archives
- Graduate art history research and batch extraction of portrait details for thematic analysis in academic publications
- Auction house provenance verification and authenticity checks using cross-referenced Met Museum accession metadata
- Virtual tour application development and real-time retrieval of portrait metadata for enhanced visitor engagement

import requests

import time

print('Objective: Find artwork title, artist, subject, and complete metadata\n')

accession_number = '29.100.5'
print(f'Searching for accession number: {accession_number}')

# First, try to access the Met Museum's official collection database directly
print('Step 1: Attempting direct access to Met Museum collection database...')

]

'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36'
}

try:
response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
print(f'Response status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
print(f'✓ Successfully accessed {url}')

# Save the response for analysis
filename = f'workspace/met_direct_search_{i+1}.html'

# Check if it's JSON or HTML
try:
json_data = response.json()
filename = f'workspace/met_api_response_{i+1}.json'
with open(filename, 'w') as f:
json.dump(json_data, f, indent=2)
print(f' Saved JSON response to: {filename}')
print(f' JSON keys: {list(json_data.keys()) if isinstance(json_data, dict) else "List with " + str(len(json_data)) + " items"}')
except:
# It's HTML
with open(filename, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)
print(f' Saved HTML response to: {filename}')

# Quick analysis of HTML content
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser')
title = soup.find('title')
title_text = title.get_text().strip() if title else 'No title found'
print(f' Page title: {title_text}')

# Look for accession number mentions
content_text = response.text.lower()
if accession_number in content_text:
print(' *** ACCESSION NUMBER FOUND IN CONTENT ***')

# Look for portrait/artwork indicators
artwork_indicators = ['portrait', 'painting', 'artist', 'artwork', 'collection']
found_indicators = [ind for ind in artwork_indicators if ind in content_text]
if found_indicators:
print(f' Artwork indicators found: {found_indicators}')

met_results.append({
'url': url,
'status': response.status_code,
'filename': filename,
'content_length': len(response.text)
})

else:
print(f'✗ Failed - Status: {response.status_code}')
met_results.append({
'url': url,
'status': response.status_code,
'error': f'HTTP {response.status_code}'
})

except Exception as e:
print(f'✗ Error: {str(e)}')
met_results.append({
'url': url,
'error': str(e)
})

time.sleep(2) # Be respectful to servers

print(f'\n=== MET MUSEUM DIRECT SEARCH RESULTS ===\n')
print(f'Attempted {len(met_collection_urls)} direct Met Museum URLs')
successful_met = [r for r in met_results if r.get('status') == 200]
print(f'Successful responses: {len(successful_met)}')

for result in successful_met:
print(f' ✓ {result["url"]} -> {result["filename"]}')

# Now use Google Search API for comprehensive search
api_key = os.getenv("SERPAPI_API_KEY")

if api_key:
print('\n=== GOOGLE SEARCH FOR MET PORTRAIT 29.100.5 ===\n')

# Multiple search queries to maximize information gathering
search_queries = [
f'Metropolitan Museum Art {accession_number} accession portrait',
f'Met Museum {accession_number} painting artwork collection',
f'"{accession_number}" Metropolitan Museum portrait artist subject',
f'metmuseum.org {accession_number} accession number artwork'
]

google_results = []

for i, query in enumerate(search_queries):
print(f'Search {i+1}: "{query}"')

params = {
"q": query,
"api_key": api_key,
"engine": "google",
"google_domain": "google.com",
"safe": "off",
"num": 8
}

try:
response = requests.get("https://serpapi.com/search.json", params=params)

if response.status_code == 200:
results = response.json()

if results.get("organic_results"):
print(f' Found {len(results["organic_results"])} results')

for j, result in enumerate(results["organic_results"]):
title = result.get('title', 'No title')
link = result.get('link', 'No link')
snippet = result.get('snippet', 'No snippet')

print(f'\n Result {j+1}:')
print(f' Title: {title}')
print(f' URL: {link}')
print(f' Snippet: {snippet}')

# Check for key information
combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower()

key_findings = []
if accession_number in combined_text:
key_findings.append('Accession number found')
if 'portrait' in combined_text:
key_findings.append('Portrait mentioned')
if 'artist' in combined_text or 'painter' in combined_text:
key_findings.append('Artist information')
if 'metmuseum.org' in link:
key_findings.append('Official Met Museum source')

if key_findings:
print(f' *** KEY FINDINGS: {key_findings} ***')

google_results.append({
'search_query': query,
'result_index': j+1,
'title': title,
'link': link,
'snippet': snippet,
'key_findings': key_findings
})
else:
print(' No organic results found')
else:
print(f' Search failed with status: {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f' Search error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(1) # Rate limiting

# Save all Google search results
with open('workspace/met_29_100_5_google_results.json', 'w') as f:
json.dump(google_results, f, indent=2)

print(f'\nGoogle search results saved to: workspace/met_29_100_5_google_results.json')
print(f'Total Google results collected: {len(google_results)}')

# Identify most promising results
priority_results = [r for r in google_results if r['key_findings']]
print(f'Priority results with key findings: {len(priority_results)}')

else:
print('\nNo SERPAPI key available - skipping Google search')
google_results = []

# Compile initial research summary
research_summary = {
'target_accession': accession_number,
'museum': 'Metropolitan Museum of Art',
'search_timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
'direct_met_searches': {
'attempted_urls': len(met_collection_urls),
'successful_responses': len(successful_met),
'results': met_results
},
'google_searches': {
'queries_attempted': len(search_queries) if api_key else 0,
'total_results': len(google_results),
'priority_results': len([r for r in google_results if r.get('key_findings')]) if google_results else 0
},
'files_created': [
f for f in os.listdir('workspace')
if f.startswith('met_') and (f.endswith('.html') or f.endswith('.json'))
]
}

with open('workspace/met_portrait_research_summary.json', 'w') as f:
json.dump(research_summary, f, indent=2)

print(f'\n=== PHASE 1 RESEARCH COMPLETE ===\n')
print(f'Research summary saved to: workspace/met_portrait_research_summary.json')
print(f'Files created in workspace: {len(research_summary["files_created"])}')
print(f'Next step: Analyze collected data to extract portrait details')

# Quick preview of findings
if successful_met:
print(f'\n✓ Successfully accessed {len(successful_met)} Met Museum URLs')
if google_results:

### Development Step 3: Search Emily Midkiff’s June 2014 Dragon Depiction Article in Fafnir Journal

**Description**: Search for information about Emily Midkiff's June 2014 article, focusing on identifying the journal named after one of Hreidmar's sons from Norse mythology. Research Hreidmar's sons (Fafnir, Regin, and Otr) to determine which one has a journal named after them, then locate Midkiff's specific article from June 2014 that discusses dragon depictions and contains quotes from two different authors expressing distaste.

**Use Cases**:
- Academic historian automating workspace inspection of downloaded HTML and JSON files to locate Emily Midkiff’s June 2014 article in the Fafnir journal for a dragon iconography dissertation
- University librarian auditing digital collections to identify and retrieve missing June 2014 issues of the mythologically named “Fafnir Journal,” updating the library management system
- Digital humanities research team extracting distaste-filled author quotations on dragon depictions from Emily Midkiff’s June 2014 paper using Python and BeautifulSoup for a folklore database
- Game development studio scraping and analyzing academic journal content on Norse mythology to inform realistic dragon design, automating extraction of relevant passages from the Fafnir journal
- Academic publisher quality control specialist validating JSON metadata against HTML search results to ensure June 2014 articles are correctly indexed in digital archives of mythologically themed journals
- Graduate student in medieval studies performing text mining on archived web pages to cross-reference Hreidmar’s sons’ journals and compile a literature review on dragon portrayals
- Museum exhibition curator automating the identification of scholarly articles in the Fafnir journal that critique dragon art to curate a thematic display on Norse mythological creatures
- Legal IP compliance team scanning downloaded HTML and JSON records to identify journals named after mythological figures and verify no trademark conflicts with a new “Fafnir” product line

```
import os
import json

print('=== INSPECTING WORKSPACE FOR PREVIOUS SEARCH RESULTS ===')
print('Objective: Review saved search data and fix technical issues to find Emily Midkiff article')
print('Target: Journal named after Hreidmar\'s son (Fafnir, Regin, or Otr) containing June 2014 article\n')

# Check workspace contents
workspace = 'workspace'
if not os.path.exists(workspace):
print('No workspace directory found, creating...')
os.makedirs(workspace)
else:
print('=== WORKSPACE CONTENTS ===')
files = os.listdir(workspace)
print(f'Total files: {len(files)}')

# Categorize files
html_files = [f for f in files if f.endswith('.html')]
json_files = [f for f in files if f.endswith('.json')]
other_files = [f for f in files if not f.endswith('.html') and not f.endswith('.json')]

print(f'HTML files: {len(html_files)}')
for html_file in html_files:
file_path = os.path.join(workspace, html_file)
file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)
print(f' - {html_file} ({file_size:,} bytes)')

print(f'JSON files: {len(json_files)}')
for json_file in json_files:
file_path = os.path.join(workspace, json_file)
file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)
print(f' - {json_file} ({file_size:,} bytes)')

if other_files:
print(f'Other files: {len(other_files)}')
for other_file in other_files:
print(f' - {other_file}')

# Inspect JSON files first to understand structure
if json_files:

try:

data = json.load(f)

print('File structure:')
if isinstance(data, dict):
for key, value in data.items():
print(f' {key}: {type(value).__name__}')
if isinstance(value, dict):
print(f' Keys: {list(value.keys())[:5]}...' if len(value.keys()) > 5 else f' Keys: {list(value.keys())}')
elif isinstance(value, list):
print(f' Length: {len(value)}')
if value and isinstance(value[0], dict):
print(f' Sample keys: {list(value[0].keys())}')
elif isinstance(value, str):
print(f' Value: {value[:100]}...' if len(value) > 100 else f' Value: {value}')
else:
print(f' Root type: {type(data).__name__}')
except Exception as e:
print(f' Error reading {json_file}: {str(e)}')

# Now inspect HTML files to see what search results we have
if html_files:
print('\n=== ANALYZING HTML SEARCH RESULTS ===')

# Import BeautifulSoup properly this time
try:
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
print('✓ BeautifulSoup imported successfully')
except ImportError:
print('✗ BeautifulSoup not available, will do text analysis instead')
BeautifulSoup = None

for html_file in html_files:
print(f'\n--- {html_file} ---')
file_path = os.path.join(workspace, html_file)

try:
with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
content = f.read()

print(f'File size: {len(content):,} characters')

# Determine what this search was for based on filename
search_type = 'unknown'
if 'fafnir' in html_file.lower():
search_type = 'Fafnir journal search'
elif 'midkiff' in html_file.lower():
search_type = 'Emily Midkiff search'
elif 'combined' in html_file.lower():
search_type = 'Combined search'

print(f'Search type: {search_type}')

# Text analysis for key terms
content_lower = content.lower()
key_terms = {
'fafnir': content_lower.count('fafnir'),
'regin': content_lower.count('regin'),
'otr': content_lower.count('otr'),
'midkiff': content_lower.count('midkiff'),
'emily': content_lower.count('emily'),
'journal': content_lower.count('journal'),
'dragon': content_lower.count('dragon'),
'2014': content_lower.count('2014'),
'june': content_lower.count('june')
}

print('Key term occurrences:')
for term, count in key_terms.items():
if count > 0:
print(f' {term}: {count}')

# Look for promising patterns
promising_patterns = [
'fafnir journal',
'regin journal',
'emily midkiff',
'midkiff 2014',
'dragon depictions',
'distaste',
'norse mythology'
]

found_patterns = []
for pattern in promising_patterns:
if pattern in content_lower:
found_patterns.append(pattern)

if found_patterns:
print(f'Promising patterns found: {found_patterns}')

# If BeautifulSoup is available, do proper HTML parsing
if BeautifulSoup:
soup = BeautifulSoup(content, 'html.parser')

# Look for result links
links = soup.find_all('a', href=True)
relevant_links = []

for link in links:
href = link.get('href', '')
text = link.get_text().strip()

if text and len(text) > 10:
# Score relevance
relevance_score = 0
text_lower = text.lower()
href_lower = href.lower()

# Check for key terms
for term in ['fafnir', 'regin', 'midkiff', 'dragon', 'journal', '2014']:
if term in text_lower:
relevance_score += 2
if term in href_lower:
relevance_score += 1

# Bonus for academic domains
academic_indicators = ['.edu', 'academia', 'jstor', 'muse', 'oxford', 'cambridge', 'taylor', 'sage']
if any(indicator in href_lower for indicator in academic_indicators):
relevance_score += 3

if relevance_score >= 2:
relevant_links.append({
'text': text[:150],
'href': href,
'score': relevance_score
})

# Sort by relevance
relevant_links.sort(key=lambda x: x['score'], reverse=True)

if relevant_links:
print(f'Found {len(relevant_links)} relevant links:')
for i, link in enumerate(relevant_links[:5], 1):
print(f' {i}. Score {link["score"]}: {link["text"]}...')
print(f' URL: {link["href"][:100]}...')
else:
print('No highly relevant links found in this search result')

# Extract text snippets around key terms for context
if 'fafnir' in content_lower and 'journal' in content_lower:
print('\n*** POTENTIAL FAFNIR JOURNAL REFERENCE ***')
fafnir_index = content_lower.find('fafnir')
if fafnir_index != -1:
start = max(0, fafnir_index - 200)
end = min(len(content), fafnir_index + 300)
context = content[start:end]
print(f'Context: ...{context}...')

if 'midkiff' in content_lower:
print('\n*** EMILY MIDKIFF REFERENCE ***')
midkiff_index = content_lower.find('midkiff')
if midkiff_index != -1:
start = max(0, midkiff_index - 200)
end = min(len(content), midkiff_index + 300)
context = content[start:end]
print(f'Context: ...{context}...')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error analyzing {html_file}: {str(e)}')

print('\n=== HREIDMAR\'S SONS RESEARCH SUMMARY ===')
print('Norse mythology: Hreidmar had three sons:')
print('1. Fafnir - Transformed into a dragon, most famous in Norse mythology')
print('2. Regin - Dwarf smith, foster father of Sigurd')
print('3. Otr - Could transform into an otter, killed by Loki')
print('\nObjective: Find which son has an academic journal named after them')
print('Target: Emily Midkiff\'s June 2014 article in that journal about dragon depictions')
print('\n=== WORKSPACE INSPECTION COMPLETE ===')

First, inspect workspace directory to understand available data workspace_dir = 'workspace' if os.path.exists(workspace_dir): files = os.listdir(workspace_dir) print(f'Files in workspace: {files}\n') # Look for files related to Whitney Museum or accession 2022.128 relevant_files = [] for filename in files: filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename) print(f'Inspecting: {filename}') if filename.endswith('.json'): print(' File type: JSON') try: with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print(f' Structure: {type(data).__name__}') if isinstance(data, dict): print(f' Keys: {list(data.keys())}') # Check for Whitney Museum or accession number references content_str = json.dumps(data, default=str).lower() if '2022.128' in content_str or 'whitney' in content_str or 'calder' in content_str: print(' *** CONTAINS RELEVANT ARTWORK DATA ***') relevant_files.append(filename) # Show key fields that might contain artwork details for key, value in data.items(): if isinstance(value, str) and len(value) < 200: print(f' {key}: {value}') elif isinstance(value, dict): print(f' {key}: Dictionary with {len(value)} keys') elif isinstance(value, list): print(f' {key}: List with {len(value)} items') else: print(f' {key}: {type(value).__name__}') elif isinstance(data, list): print(f' Length: {len(data)} items') if data and isinstance(data[0], dict): print(f' Sample keys: {list(data[0].keys())}') # Check first few items for relevant content for i, item in enumerate(data[:3]): item_str = json.dumps(item, default=str).lower() if '2022.128' in item_str or 'whitney' in item_str or 'calder' in item_str: print(f' *** ITEM {i} CONTAINS RELEVANT DATA ***') relevant_files.append(filename) break except Exception as e: print(f' Error reading JSON: {e}') elif filename.endswith('.html'): print(' File type: HTML') try: with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: html_content = f.read() print(f' Content length: {len(html_content)} characters') # Check for accession number or relevant terms content_lower = html_content.lower() if '2022.128' in content_lower: print(' *** CONTAINS ACCESSION NUMBER 2022.128 ***') relevant_files.append(filename) if 'calder' in content_lower: print(' *** CONTAINS CALDER REFERENCE ***') if 'juggler' in content_lower: print(' *** CONTAINS JUGGLER REFERENCE ***') if 'book' in content_lower: print(' *** CONTAINS BOOK REFERENCE ***') except Exception as e: print(f' Error reading HTML: {e}') print() print(f'=== RELEVANT FILES IDENTIFIED: {len(relevant_files)} ===\n') for rf in relevant_files: print(f' - {rf}') # Based on tester feedback, focus on the two key files with detailed descriptions workspace_dir = 'workspace' key_files = [ 'whitney_2022_128_complete_metadata.json', 'whitney_2022_128_final_summary.txt' ] print('=== EXAMINING COMPLETE METADATA FILE ===\n') metadata_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'whitney_2022_128_complete_metadata.json') if os.path.exists(metadata_file): # First inspect the structure safely with open(metadata_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: metadata = json.load(f) print('File structure inspection:') print(f'Root keys: {list(metadata.keys())}') # Examine extracted_metadata section which likely contains detailed descriptions if 'extracted_metadata' in metadata: extracted = metadata['extracted_metadata'] print(f'\nExtracted metadata keys: {list(extracted.keys())}') # Look for description fields description_fields = [] for key, value in extracted.items(): print(f'\n{key}:') print(f' Type: {type(value)}') if isinstance(value, list): print(f' Length: {len(value)}') if value: print(f' Sample: {str(value[0])[:200]}...') # Check if this contains detailed descriptions if any(desc_word in str(value).lower() for desc_word in ['description', 'depicts', 'shows', 'figure', 'sculpture']): description_fields.append(key) elif isinstance(value, str): print(f' Content: {value[:200]}...') if any(desc_word in value.lower() for desc_word in ['description', 'depicts', 'shows', 'figure', 'sculpture']): description_fields.append(key) elif isinstance(value, dict): print(f' Dictionary keys: {list(value.keys())}') print(f'\nIdentified description fields: {description_fields}') # Extract and analyze all text content for book/reading references print('\n=== DETAILED CONTENT ANALYSIS ===\n') all_text_content = [] for key, value in extracted.items(): print(f'--- {key.upper()} ---') if isinstance(value, list): for i, item in enumerate(value): if isinstance(item, str) and len(item) > 50: # Focus on substantial text print(f'Item {i+1}: {item}') all_text_content.append(item) # Check for book/reading references item_lower = item.lower() book_indicators = ['book', 'reading', 'text', 'page', 'manuscript', 'holding'] found_indicators = [ind for ind in book_indicators if ind in item_lower] if found_indicators: print(f' *** BOOK/READING INDICATORS: {found_indicators} ***') # Check for figure/person descriptions figure_indicators = ['person', 'figure', 'human', 'man', 'woman', 'juggler', 'performer'] found_figures = [ind for ind in figure_indicators if ind in item_lower] if found_figures: print(f' *** FIGURE INDICATORS: {found_figures} ***') elif isinstance(value, str) and len(value) > 50: print(f'Content: {value}') all_text_content.append(value) # Check for book/reading references value_lower = value.lower() book_indicators = ['book', 'reading', 'text', 'page', 'manuscript', 'holding'] found_indicators = [ind for ind in book_indicators if ind in value_lower] if found_indicators: print(f' *** BOOK/READING INDICATORS: {found_indicators} ***') # Also check source_details for additional context if 'source_details' in metadata: print('\n=== SOURCE DETAILS ANALYSIS ===\n') sources = metadata['source_details'] for i, source in enumerate(sources): print(f'Source {i+1}:') if isinstance(source, dict): for key, value in source.items(): if isinstance(value, str) and len(value) > 100: print(f' {key}: {value[:300]}...') # Check for visual descriptions value_lower = value.lower() if 'book' in value_lower and ('hold' in value_lower or 'reading' in value_lower): print(f' *** POTENTIAL BOOK HOLDING DESCRIPTION ***') print() else: print(f'Metadata file not found: {metadata_file}') print('\n=== EXAMINING FINAL SUMMARY FILE ===\n') summary_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, 'whitney_2022_128_final_summary.txt') if os.path.exists(summary_file): with open(summary_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: summary_content = f.read() print(f'Summary file length: {len(summary_content)} characters') print('\nSummary content:') print(summary_content) # A juggler would typically be shown with juggling objects, not reading material') print('\nCONCLUSION PENDING: Awaiting detailed description analysis...')
